<user_name>Kym McKenna< /user_name>< review>
Myself and 3 friends went to Tu Madre last night for an early dinner at 4:30. We ordered the guacamole and chips and the Ahi wontons. The Guacamole tasted nice but there were literally only about 2 tablespoons and a large handful of chips served for $10. We all had margaritas which were $11 on happy hour price and what we all got was a tumbler full of ice. 2 of us wanted to order the chicken enchiladas but we were told they were "all out" of them. At 4:30 ? I would think the enchiladas are probably a mainstay of a Mexican restaurant. I ordered a mexi/cobb salad, 1 person ordered the carnitas and 2 ordered the pulpo. We all left the restaurant feeling hungry. Our bill for 2 rounds of drinks, 2 appetizers and 4 main courses was $150 not including a tip. While the food is fresh, the portion sizes are ridiculously small for the prices they are charging. The atmosphere is nice but this restaurant is not good value for money.</review>

<username>Triparadox C.< /username><Time>1610959557853</Time><Rating>5</Rating>< text>
After approximately just a shy of a year, I got a coupon and decided to have an order here. It was the Combo Pizza that pretty much had it all from pepperoni, olives, bell pepper, and some meatballs. The taste was awesome. It didn't arrive when it was hot, but it was warm enough, and the texture was still very nice. It's very nice to see that they haven't lowered the quality, as well as being generous with the toppings.

One thing that you need to understand is that this place is not for everyone. If you are tight on budget, you might want to find some other alternatives as this place will charge you a decent amount. That being said, when you are feeling generous once in a while, this place would be one of the best pizza restaurant in the city, and perhaps county.</text>

After purchasing a new mattress at the Glendale location, I discovered that Sit 'n Sleep doesn't refer to bedding, but to customer service. My wife and I purchased a new mattress in March, replacing our worn out bed, which was also purchased at Sit 'n Sleep years ago at a different location. Ali, the sales associate got us into a comfortable mattress and we made the purchase.  And that's when the problems began.  We slept on it for a week, and we both woke up sore.  The middle of the bed seemed worn down.  I called Ali and left messages and sent emails but he never replied. My wife called and finally reached him. My advice is this:  avoid Ali and the Glendale store, and if there is a problem, don't think customer service is going to help you. <Rating>5< /Rating>< review>
Delicious local hole in the wall suggested to me by a friend. The carne asada wet burritos are delicious. It's worth the extra money to get them wet, slathered in a rich tomato onion pepper sauce and covered in cheese. The beef is delicious. Many local spots the beef can taste gamey and weird. Tacos plus had great asada with an amazing flavor and you could taste the grilled magnificence. The plates come with two side chips and your choices of salsa. I ordered the rice and beans and they are so good together. When I say the burritos are huge I mean it. You could easily split one with the sides. The staff was friendly and parking was easy in the lot out front. They also made sure to abide by the current covid 19 measures. I look forward to going back and trying more of their items soon. Yum.</review>

@Sonia Fuentes, ¬°escucha menzo puta! You are the same person that would complain if someone was sitting in your reserved seat.
Your review is spoiled brat temper tantrum childish at best, and ridiculous to say the least.  :/

I've been coming to this restaurant for years. The food is da bomb. Everything I have ordered here is yummy. Even in S. California, Its usually hard to find Mexican restaurants like this that have genuine Mex food flavor. This restaurant is an exception. If the owners could find a way to put this restaurant somewhere in West L.A, they'd have so much business, there would be lines around the restaurant. Avoid the corporate Mexican chain restaurants, go to Pancho's.....way better.

Their recipes come from private home made sources

The service is not the greatest, but who cares? You want something? Just ask. It feels like family here.

They have live entertainment on the weekends and it packs the house.

The fountain drinks could be of better quality (Jamaica), but its not a problem.

Se habla Ingl√©s, y Espanol.</review>
